large (target) model autoregressive_sampling: Develop a Python program to track real-time stock market data. \ndef get_stock_data(symbol, date_range, interval):
    """
    This function will get the stock data for a given symbol from yahoo finance.
    :param symbol: stock symbol
    :param date_range: date range for the data (1d,5d,1mo,3mo,6mo,1y,2y,5y,10y,ytd,max)
    :param interval: stock data interval (1m,2m,5m,15m,30m,60m,90m,1h,1d,5d,1wk,1mo,3mo)
    :return: stock data
    """
    # get the stock data
    data = yf.download(symbol, date_range, interval)
    # return the stock data
    return data

deepmind's speculative_sampling: Develop a Python program to track real-time stock market data. \ndef get_stock_data(symbol, date_range, interval):
    """
    This function will get the stock data for a given symbol from yahoo finance.
    :param symbol: stock symbol
    :param date_range: date range for the data (1d,5d,1mo,3mo,6mo,1y,2y,5y,10y,ytd,max)
    :param interval: stock data interval (1m,2m,5m,15m,30m,60m,90m,1h,1d,5d,1wk,1mo,3mo)
    :return: stock data
    """
    # get the stock data
    data = yf.download(symbol, date_range, interval)
    # return the stock data
    return data

large (target) model autoregressive_sampling: Develop a Python program to track real-time stock market data. \ndef get_stock_data(symbol, date_range, interval):
    """
    This function will get the stock data for a given symbol from yahoo finance.
    :param symbol: stock symbol
    :param date_range: date range for the data (1d,5d,1mo,3mo,6mo,1y,2y,5y,10y,ytd,max)
    :param interval: stock data interval (1m,2m,5m,15m,30m,60m,90m,1h,1d,5d,1wk,1mo,3mo)
    :return: stock data
    """
    # get the stock data
    data = yf.download(symbol, date_range, interval)
    # return the stock data
    return data

    """
    This function will get the stock data for a given symbol from yahoo finance.
    :param symbol: stock symbol
    :param date_range: date range for the data (1d,5d,1mo,3mo,6mo,1y,2y,5y,10y,ytd,max)
    :param interval: stock data interval (1m,2m,5m,15m,30m,60m,90m,1h,1d,5d,1wk,1mo,3mo)
    :return: stock data

    # return the stock data
    return data
